                    <h2>Meet Luke Warren</h2>

                    <div class="credentials">

                        <h3>Bachelor of Music Education</h3>

                        <p>University of Tennessee, 2024</p>

                        <div style="margin-top: 15px;">

                            <strong>Experience:</strong>

                            <ul style="margin-top: 8px; padding-left: 20px;">

                                <li>Active participant in the music community since 2016</li>

                                <li>Technical staff member with Clinton High School marching band</li>

                                <li>Completed comprehensive student teaching program at Clinton High School</li>

                                <li>Extensive band directing experience including lesson planning and music selection</li>

                                <li>Proven track record in student engagement and educational development</li>

                                <li>Tennessee State certified music educator</li>

                            </ul>

                        </div>

                    </div>

                    <p>Luke brings warmth, patience, and genuine enthusiasm to every lesson. He believes that music should be both challenging and enjoyable, creating a welcoming space where students feel comfortable exploring their musical potential.</p>

                    <p style="margin-top: 1rem;"><strong>Rate:</strong> $30/hour</p>
